                'slug' => '',
                'description' => 'Firework color concoctions are comprised of different metal elements. When an element burns, its electrons get excited, and it releases energy in the form of light. Different chemicals burn at different wavelengths of light. Strontium and lithium compounds produce deep reds; copper produces blues; titanium and magnesium burn silver or white; calcium creates an orange color; sodium produces yellow pyrotechnics; and finally, barium burns green. Combining chlorine with barium or copper creates neon green and turquoise flames, respectively. Blue is apparently the most difficult to produce. Pyrotechnic stars comprised of these chemicals are typically propelled into the sky using an aerial shell.',

<p> The scientific term for brain freeze is “sphenopalatine ganglioneuralgia.”</p>
<p>Canadians say “sorry” so much that a law was passed in 2009 declaring that an apology can’t be used as evidence of admission to guilt.</p>

<p>Daniel Radcliffe was allergic to his Harry Potter glasses.</p>
<p>He had an allergy to nickel, and they were quickly replaced with hypoallergenic specs.</p>
<p>Also, did you know that his glasses had no lenses? This was to prevent reflections from anything happening behind the scenes. The glass lens was added in post-production.</p>

<p>The largest snowflake in the world was found in 1887 it was 15 inches wide and 8 inches thick.</p>

<p>Enceladus, one of Saturn’s smaller moons, reflects 90% of the sunlight, making it more reflective than snow.</p>

<p>In India, the flying of a kite is illegal under a 1934 law, which classes kites as aircraft.</p>

<p>“Finger Lickin’ Good” had a bit of a mishap when translated to Chinese for their first KFC outlets in the country, the famous phrase became “eat your fingers off.”</p>
<p>Giraffe hearts pump twice as hard as a cow’s heart in order to get blood to its brain.</p>

<p>In feudal Japan, lords purposely built homes with squeaky floors as a defensive measure against ninjas.</p>
<p>In 2015, Ariana Grande won two MTV Millennial Awards for the “Global Instagrammer of the Year” and “International Hit of the Year” with her single “One Last Time.”</p>
<p>The word “peacock” does not actually apply to both male and female birds. It’s only the males that are called peacocks, while the females are called peahens. Together, the collective name for them is “peafowl.”</p>
<p>Evangeline Lilly is a notoriously bad driver. She has been in at least 8 car accidents, and none of them were with another car.</p>
<p>In 1993, Aleksandr A. Serebrov took his Game Boy to space. Later, it was auctioned for $1,220 and is said to have orbited earth 3,000 times.</p>
<p>The patterns on a giraffe are totally unique - no two giraffes are ever the same.</p>
<p>Geomelophagia is someone who has the urge to eat raw potatoes.</p>
<p>Drink green tea before bed to burn calories while sleeping. Green tea will also increase your metabolism.</p>

<p>Legoland Billund opened on June 7, 1968, and attracted over 3,000 visitors on the first day!</p>
<p>The state vegetable of Oklahoma is the Watermelon, despite the fact that it is indeed a fruit.</p>
<p>In 1911, Bobby Leach was the 2nd person to go over Niagara Falls in a barrel. He died 15 years later from slipping on an orange peel and getting gangrene.</p>
<p>In Texas, according to Texas Parks and Wildlife Department, it is legal to kill Bigfoot if you find it. It would be considered a non-protected nongame animal.</p>
<p>In 1922 &amp; 1933, The Coca-Cola Company was offered a chance to buy the Pepsi-Cola company, and it declined on three separate occasions.</p>

<p>The Earth is the only planet in our solar system not named after either a Greek or Roman God.</p>

<p>The most leaves ever found on a single clover is 56.</p>
<p>There is actually a difference between coffins and caskets - coffins are typically tapered and six-sided, while caskets are rectangular.</p>

<p>More than 45 million turkeys are cooked and eaten in the U.S. at Thanksgiving.</p>
<p>Li&egrave;ge, Belgium, tried to use 37 cats to deliver mail in the 1870s. Most of the cats took up to a day to deliver the mail, and the service was short-lived.</p>
<p>A female’s heart is smaller than a male’s by about 25%. Because of this, the female heart has to beat around six times more than the male heart to pump the correct amount of blood around the body.</p>
<p>In 1325, two Italian city states fought over a bucket, which resulted in 2,000 deaths. It started when two soldiers stole a bucket from a well in the city center.</p>
<p>In 2000 the first permanent crew inhabited the International Space Station (ISS). Since then, there’s always been a human presence in space.</p>
<p>Turkey vultures use defensive vomit to get rid of any disturbing animal. They can propel their vomit up to 10 feet.</p>
<p>During World War II, the very first bomb dropped on Berlin by the Allies killed the only elephant in Berlin Zoo.</p>
<p>Peaches are the third most popular fruit grown in America.</p>
<p>Emilie de Ravin&lsquo;s biggest TV role as Claire Littleton on the hit show “Lost“, loves peanut butter - which is unintentionally ironic because Emilie is allergic to peanuts. In reality, her biggest weakness is actually chocolate.</p>
<p>Jupiter has 69 moons. A few are 12-37 miles in diameter, but most are barely 1 mile in size. Jupiter itself is 317 times the mass of the Earth.</p>

<p>Losing Weight is the most common New Year’s resolution.</p>

<p>The smallest possible measurement of length is known as the Planck Length. Anything smaller than this would break everything we understand about physics.</p>
<p>The social media website, MySpace, was founded in 2003 and sold for $580 million in 2005. At this time, it was the most visited social networking site in the world and even surpassed Google as the most visited website in the United States!</p>
<p>One of the earliest depictions of dreadlocks dates back to 1600 BC to the Minoan Civilization, one of Europe’s earliest civilizations, who lived in what is now known as Greece.</p>

<p>Polygamy is the practice of having more than one husband or wife at the same time. Polygyny is when a man is married to more than one woman, and Polyandry is when a woman is married to more than one husband.</p>
<p>As of September 2016, the Giant Panda was downgraded from “endangered” to “vulnerable” on the Global List of Species at Risk of Extinction.</p>
<p>The world’s oldest surviving bank is “Banca Monte dei Paschi di Siena,” which was founded in 1472 and is currently Italy’s 3rd largest bank.</p>
<p>The letter Z is the least frequently used letter in written English. It is more common in American English than in British English due to spelling differences.</p>
<p>The cardboard holder that you often get around a takeaway cup of coffee is called a “zarf.”</p>
<p>The logo for the Monster energy drink cans is not an M, as most believe, but are claw marks from a monster ripping through the can. In 2014 a YouTube video gained an international audience when they claimed that each segment of the claw mark looks like the Hebrew symbol for the number six, making the logo into 666, the number of the Beast.</p>
<p>The largest pumpkin pie ever baked was in 2005 and weighed 2,020 pounds or just over 916kg.</p>
<p>The Triangle took nearly 100 years to become a popular orchestral instrument.</p>
<p>The first computer virus ever created was called Creeper back in 1971. Shortly after this virus was created, Reaper was created as the world’s first anti-virus.</p>
<p>The earliest mention of the mythical creature, the Unicorn, dates back as far as 2700 BC in Asia and was described as a creature of great power and wisdom.</p>
<p>The oldest webcam stream online today is The San Francisco FogCam which has been operational since 1994.</p>
<p>In Japanese legend, it is said that anyone who folds 1,000 origami cranes will be granted a wish by the gods.</p>
<p>Doggerland is the area of land connecting Great Britain to continental Europe. It was flooded by rising sea levels (6500-6200 BC), turning Great Britain into an island.</p>
